4634
4635/* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function. */
4636#define CHARSET_NAME "EUC-JP-MS//"
4637#define FROM_LOOP from_eucjp_ms
4638#define TO_LOOP to_eucjp_ms
4639#define DEFINE_INIT 1
4640#define DEFINE_FINI 1
4641#define MIN_NEEDED_FROM 1
4642#define MAX_NEEDED_FROM 3
4643#define MIN_NEEDED_TO 4
4644#define ONE_DIRECTION 0
4645
4646
4647/* First define the conversion function from EUC-JP-MS to UCS4. */
4648#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4649#define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4650#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
4651#define LOOPFCT FROM_LOOP
4652#define BODY \
4653 { \
4654 uint32_t ch = (uint32_t)inptr[0] & 0xff; \
4655 \
4656 if (ch < 0x8e || (ch >= 0x90 && ch <= 0x9f)) \
4657 ++inptr; \
4658 else if (ch == 0xff) \
4659 { \
4660 /* This is illegal. */ \
4661 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4662 { \
4663 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4664 break; \
4665 } \
4666 \
4667 ++inptr; \
4668 ++*irreversible; \
4669 continue; \
4670 } \
4671 else \
4672 { \
4673 /* Two or more byte character. First test whether the next \
4674 character is also available. */ \
4675 unsigned char ch2; \
4676 \
4677 if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend)) \
4678 { \
4679 /* The second character is not available. Store the \
4680 intermediate result. */ \
4681 result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT; \
4682 break; \
4683 } \
4684 \
4685 ch2 = (unsigned char)inptr[1]; \
4686 \
4687 /* All second bytes of a multibyte character must be >= 0xa1. */ \
4688 if (__glibc_unlikely (ch2 < 0xa1)) \
4689 { \
4690 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4691 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4692 { \
4693 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4694 break; \
4695 } \
4696 \
4697 ++inptr; \
4698 ++*irreversible; \
4699 continue; \
4700 } \
4701 \
4702 if (__builtin_expect(ch == 0x8e, 0)) \
4703 { \
4704 /* This is code set 2: half-width katakana. */ \
4705 ch = jisx0201_to_ucs4 (ch2); \
4706 /*if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR)*/ \
4707 if (__glibc_unlikely (ch == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR)) \
4708 { \
4709 /* Illegal character. */ \
4710 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4711 { \
4712 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4713 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4714 break; \
4715 } \
4716 } \
4717 \
4718 inptr += 2; \
4719 } \
4720 else \
4721 { \
4722 const unsigned char *endp = inptr; \
4723 int mblen = 1; \
4724 \
4725 if (__builtin_expect(ch == 0x8f, 0)) \
4726 { \
4727 if (inend - inptr < 3) \
4728 ch = 0; \
4729 else \
4730 { \
4731 unsigned char ch3 = (unsigned char)inptr[2]; \
4732 mblen = 3; \
4733 \
4734 if (__builtin_expect(ch3 == 0xff, 0) \
4735 || __builtin_expect(ch3 < 0xa1, 0)) \
4736 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4737 else if (ch2 <= 0xf2) \
4738 { \
4739 endp = inptr + 1; \
4740 \
4741 /* This is code set 3: JIS X 0212-1990. */ \
4742 ch = jisx0212_to_ucs4 (&endp, inend - endp, 0x80); \
4743 \
4744 if (ch == 0x00a6) /* BROKEN BAR */ \
4745 ch = 0xffe4; /* FULLWIDTH BROKEN BAR */ \
4746 else if (ch == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR) \
4747 endp -= 1; \
4748 } \
4749 else if (ch2 <= 0xf4) \
4750 { \
4751 int idx = ((ch2-0xf3)*94 + ch3-0xa1) - (94-12); \
4752 \
4753 if (0 <= idx && idx < 12 + 94) \
4754 { \
4755 if ((ch = cjk_block_ibm[idx]) != 0) \
4756 endp = inptr + mblen; \
4757 else \
4758 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4759 } \
4760 else \
4761 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4762 } \
4763 else if (ch2 <= 0xfe) \
4764 { \
4765 ch = 0xe3ac + (ch2 - 0xf5) * 94 + (ch3 - 0xa1); \
4766 endp = inptr + mblen; \
4767 } \
4768 else \
4769 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4770 } \
4771 } \
4772 else if (__builtin_expect(0xa1 <= ch, 1)) \
4773 { \
4774 mblen = 2; \
4775 \
4776 if (inend - inptr < 2) \
4777 ch = 0; \
4778 else if (__builtin_expect(ch2 == 0xff, 0)) \
4779 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4780 else if (ch <= 0xa8) \
4781 { \
4782 if ((ch = cjk_block1[(ch-0xa1)*94 + (ch2-0xa1)]) != 0) \
4783 endp = inptr + mblen; \
4784 else \
4785 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4786 } \
4787 else if (ch == 0xad) \
4788 { \
4789 if ((ch = cjk_block2[(ch-0xad)*94 + (ch2-0xa1)]) != 0) \
4790 endp = inptr + mblen; \
4791 else \
4792 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4793 } \
4794 else if (ch <= 0xf4) \
4795 { \
4796 endp = inptr; \
4797 \
4798 /* This is code set 1: JIS X 0208. */ \
4799 ch = jisx0208_to_ucs4 (&endp, inend - inptr, 0x80); \
4800 } \
4801 else if (ch <= 0xfe) \
4802 { \
4803 ch = 0xe000 + (ch - 0xf5) * 94 + (ch2 - 0xa1); \
4804 endp = inptr + mblen; \
4805 } \
4806 else \
4807 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4808 } \
4809 else \
4810 ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR; \
4811 \
4812 if (__builtin_expect (ch, 1) == 0) \
4813 { \
4814 /* Not enough input available. */ \
4815 result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT; \
4816 break; \
4817 } \
4818 if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR) \
4819 { \
4820 /* Illegal character. */ \
4821 if (! ignore_errors_p ()) \
4822 { \
4823 /* This is an illegal character. */ \
4824 result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT; \
4825 break; \
4826 } \
4827 \
4828 inptr += mblen; \
4829 ++*irreversible; \
4830 continue; \
4831 } \
4832 inptr = endp; \
4833 } \
4834 } \
4835 \
4836 put32 (outptr, ch); \
4837 outptr += 4; \
4838 }
4839#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4840#include <iconv/loop.c>
4841
4842
4843/* Next, define the other direction. */
4844#define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT MIN_NEEDED_TO
4845#define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4846#define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4847#define LOOPFCT TO_LOOP
4848#define BODY \
4849 { \
4850 uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr); \
4851 const unsigned char *cp; \
4852 unsigned char pua[2]; \
4853 \
4854 if (ch >= (sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1) / sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1[0]))) \
4855 { \
4856 if (ch >= 0x0100 && ch <= 0x045f) \
4857 cp = from_ucs4_greek[ch - 0x0100]; \
4858 else if (ch >= 0x2010 && ch <= 0x9fa5) \
4859 cp = from_ucs4_cjk[ch - 0x2010]; \
4860 else if (ch >= 0xe000 && ch <= 0xe757) \
4861 { \
4862 if (ch < 0xe3ac) \
4863 { \
4864 pua[0] = (ch - 0xe000) / 94 + 0xf5; \
4865 pua[1] = (ch - 0xe000) % 94 + 0xa1; \
4866 } \
4867 else \
4868 { \
4869 pua[0] = (ch - 0xe3ac) / 94 + 0xf5; \
4870 pua[1] = (ch - 0xe3ac) % 94 + 0x21; \
4871 } \
4872 cp = (const unsigned char *)&pua[0]; \
4873 } \
4874 else if (ch >= 0xf929 && ch <= 0xfa2d) \
4875 cp = from_ucs4_cjkcpt[ch - 0xf929]; \
4876 else if (__builtin_expect (ch >= 0xff01, 1) \
4877 && __builtin_expect (ch <= 0xffe5, 1)) \
4878 cp = from_ucs4_extra[ch - 0xff01]; \
4879 else \
4880 { \
4881 UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4); \
4882 /* Illegal character. */ \
4883 cp = (const unsigned char *) ""; \
4884 } \
4885 } \
4886 else \
4887 cp = from_ucs4_lat1[ch]; \
4888 \
4889 if (__builtin_expect (cp[0], '\1') == '\0' && ch != 0) \
4890 { \
4891 /* Illegal character. */ \
4892 STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4); \
4893 } \
4894 else \
4895 { \
4896 *outptr = cp[0]; \
4897 /* Now test for a possible second byte and write this if possible. */\
4898 if (cp[1] != '\0') \
4899 { \
4900 if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend)) \
4901 { \
4902 /* The result does not fit into the buffer. */ \
4903 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
4904 break; \
4905 } \
4906 if (__glibc_unlikely (cp[1] < 0x80)) \
4907 { \
4908 if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 2 >= outend)) \
4909 { \
4910 /* The result does not fit into the buffer. */ \
4911 result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT; \
4912 break; \
4913 } \
4914 *outptr = 0x8f; \
4915 *++outptr = cp[0]; \
4916 *++outptr = cp[1] | 0x80; \
4917 } \
4918 else \
4919 *++outptr = cp[1]; \
4920 } \
4921 ++outptr; \
4922 } \
4923 \
4924 inptr += 4; \
4925 }
4926#define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4927#include <iconv/loop.c>
